  ---
  Industry Tools for Prompt Engineering

  Tier 1 вҖ” Highest Relevance for Your Stack

  Tool: promptfoo
  What It Does: CI-based prompt testing & regression detection. Define test
  cases
    in YAML, run assertions against LLM output (JSON schema validation,
    contains/not-contains, custom JS assertions). Open-source, free.
  Why It Fits: Test all 7 action types with expected outputs. Catch regressions
    when you edit prompts. Works with Qwen/DeepSeek via OpenAI-compatible API.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Tool: Langfuse
  What It Does: Prompt versioning, tracing, observability. Self-hostable (MIT
    license), supports prompt templates with variables.
  Why It Fits: Version your .md prompts, track which version produced which
    outputs. Self-hosted = medical data stays on your infra.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Tool: Instructor
  What It Does: Structured output enforcement via Pydantic models. You already
    use this.
  Why It Fits: Validated approach вҖ” research shows JSON schema enforcement >
    prompt-only schema instructions for Chinese LLMs.

  ---
  Key Research Findings for Your Domain

  1. CoT Paradox in Medical NLP

  2025 research shows Chain-of-Thought reduces accuracy in 86% of clinical 
  extraction tasks (NER, field extraction, classification). CoT helps only for
  reasoning-heavy tasks (differential diagnosis, treatment planning).

  For your prompts: Your doctor-extract.md and patient-extract.md correctly use
  /no_think (zero-shot extraction). Your diagnosis.md should use CoT/thinking
  mode. This split is validated.

  2. Qwen3 Prompting Best Practices

  - /no_think for extraction tasks (structured output, field extraction) вҖ”
  you're already doing this
  - /think (default) for reasoning tasks (diagnosis, treatment planning)
  - System prompts work well in Qwen3 вҖ” use them for role definition and
  constraints
  - Never use greedy decoding (temperature=0) with Qwen3 thinking mode

  3. Chinese vs English Prompting

  - Chinese prompts on Chinese-trained models (Qwen, DeepSeek) perform equal or
  better than English
  - Best pattern for your case: Chinese for medical content/patient-facing, keep
   technical schema instructions in Chinese too since your entire pipeline is
  Chinese
  - Medical abbreviations (STEMI, BNP, CT, MRI) should stay in English вҖ” your
  system/base.md already handles this correctly

  4. Prompt Caching Strategy

  For Qwen3/DeepSeek with API providers that support KV cache:
  - Static prefix: system prompt + SOAP schema + rules + examples (cacheable)
  - Dynamic suffix: patient data, conversation history (per-request)
  - Structure prompts so the long, stable part comes first

  ---
  Actionable Recommendations (Priority Order)

  1. Add examples to bare prompts вҖ” doctor-extract.md, patient-extract.md,
  create-task.md, vision-ocr.md need at least 2 examples each (one normal, one
  edge case)
  2. Adopt promptfoo for regression testing вҖ” write test suites for each prompt
  with input/expected-output pairs. Run in CI before deploying prompt changes.
  3. Consolidate duplicates вҖ” decide on one canonical location for each prompt
  (root vs intent/), symlink or delete the other. Merge compose.md and query.md.
  4. Add error handling sections вҖ” each prompt should specify: what to do with
  empty input, conflicting data, insufficient information, and malformed input.
  5. Standardize prompt structure вҖ” adopt a consistent template:
  # Role (и§’иүІ)
  # Task (д»»еҠЎ)
  # Input Format (иҫ“е…Ҙж јејҸ)
  # Output Schema (иҫ“еҮәж јејҸ) вҖ” with JSON schema
  # Rules (и§„еҲҷ) вҖ” numbered, priority-ordered
  # Constraints (зәҰжқҹ) вҖ” safety/anti-hallucination
  # Examples (зӨәдҫӢ) вҖ” вүҘ2, including edge cases
  # Error Handling (ејӮеёёеӨ„зҗҶ)
  6. Add negative/adversarial examples вҖ” show the model what NOT to extract
  (greetings mixed with clinical data, ambiguous abbreviations, off-topic
  content)
  7. Version your prompts вҖ” either via Langfuse or a simpler PROMPT_VERSION
  header in each .md file with a changelog comment

  Want me to start implementing any of these? I'd suggest beginning with adding
  examples to the 4 bare prompts, or setting up a promptfoo test suite.

  Critical findings:

  1. create-task.md is structurally miswired вҖ” Handler reads
  ctx.routing.params.title/content/due_at directly, but routing.md has zero
  create_task examples showing those params. Adding examples to create-task.md
  alone won't fix production behavior.
  2. Field count drift вҖ” Extract prompts list 13 fields, but schema.py has 14
  (includes department), and comments in completeness.py/interview_summary.py
  still say "14-field."
  3. Missing edge cases in proposed examples:
    - Correction/contradiction across turns (doctor corrects earlier info)
    - Non-symptom chief complaints (жңҜеҗҺеӨҚжҹҘ3жңҲ, дҪ“жЈҖеҸ‘зҺ°иӮәз»“иҠӮ1е‘Ё)
    - Diagnosis qualifiers preserved (иҖғиҷ‘вҖҰ, еҫ…жҺ’, ?)
    - Colloquial negatives beyond literal "жІЎжңү"
  4. chief_complaint вүӨ20еӯ— should be soft вҖ” Hard constraint forces
  compression/rewriting in no-think mode. Recommend:
  "е°ҪйҮҸвүӨ20еӯ—пјҢдёҚиҰҒжңәжў°жҲӘж–ӯпјӣе…ій”®дҝЎжҒҜдјҳе…Ҳ"
  5. /no_think needs high-contrast examples вҖ” Coverage > count. 3-4 sharply
  different examples beat many repetitive ones.
  6. Relative dates unsafe вҖ” create-task examples use "дёӢе‘ЁдёҖ" but system prompt
   doesn't inject {current_date}.
  7. No Pydantic validation вҖ” raw json_mode + json.loads means prompt examples
  and schema wording matter more.

  Recommended example matrix:
  - doctor-extract: full case, dedup, correction/contradiction, AI/filtering +
  follow-up
  - patient-extract: full case, negatives, off-topic, chief_complaint vs 
  present_illness boundary
  - create-task: absolute date, no due date, content extraction, minimal
  title-only

  Revised Action Plan

  Based on all 5 reviews, here's what I'd change from the original proposal:

  1. Add 4th example to each prompt вҖ” correction/contradiction case
  2. Soften chief_complaint вҖ” "е°ҪйҮҸвүӨ20еӯ—" not hard constraint
  3. Add synonym mapping rule вҖ” expand "жІЎжңүвҶ’ж— " to include "жңӘеҸ‘зҺ°", "дёҚжё…жҘҡ"
  etc
  4. Fix create-task structural issue вҖ” either add create_task examples to
  routing.md OR wire up a second LLM call
  5. Inject {current_date} into create-task prompt
  6. Add contrastive negative in each example set вҖ” show one "do NOT extract
  this" case

  Want me to revise the proposed examples incorporating this feedback, or do you
   want to discuss any of these points first?

  Known Issue: {current_date} needs code wiring

  The {current_date} placeholder in create-task.md won't auto-substitute вҖ”
  get_prompt_sync() returns raw text without .format(). More critically, the
  handler calls datetime.fromisoformat(due_at_str) which will fail on relative 
  dates ("дёӢе‘ЁдёҖ") returned by the router. Two code fixes needed:

  1. Router side: Inject current date so routing can resolve relative вҶ’ ISO-8601
  2. Handler side: Add relative date parsing fallback (or accept the router
  passing raw strings)

  Want me to fix the code side too?

         +": 5, "ж—Ҙ": 6, "еӨ©": 6}                                        
      15 +                                                               
      16 +                                                               
      17 +def _parse_chinese_date(raw: str) -> Optional[datetime]:       
      18 +    """Best-effort parse of Chinese relative date expressions. 
      19 +                                                               
      20 +    Handles: жҳҺеӨ©, еҗҺеӨ©, дёӢе‘ЁX, дёӢдёӘжңҲ, with optional дёҠеҚҲ/дёӢеҚҲ
         +/жҷҡдёҠ time.                                                    
      21 +    Returns None if unparseable.                               
      22 +    """                                                        
      23 +    now = datetime.now()                                       
      24 +    base: Optional[datetime] = None                            
      25 +    text = raw.strip()                                         
      26 +                                                               
      27 +    # Absolute ISO-8601 вҖ” try first                            
      28 +    try:                                                       
      29 +        return datetime.fromisoformat(text)                    
      30 +    except (ValueError, TypeError):                            
      31 +        pass                                                   
      32 +                                                               
      33 +    # д»ҠеӨ©                                                     
      34 +    if text.startswith("д»ҠеӨ©"):                                
      35 +        base = now.replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsec
         +ond=0)                                                         
      36 +    # жҳҺеӨ©                                                     
      37 +    elif text.startswith("жҳҺеӨ©"):                              
      38 +        base = (now + timedelta(days=1)).replace(hour=0, minute
         +=0, second=0, microsecond=0)                                   
      39 +    # еҗҺеӨ©                                                     
      40 +    elif text.startswith("еҗҺеӨ©"):                              
      41 +        base = (now + timedelta(days=2)).replace(hour=0, minute
         +=0, second=0, microsecond=0)                                   
      42 +    # дёӢе‘ЁX                                                    
      43 +    elif m := re.match(r"дёӢе‘Ё([\u4e00-\u4e09\u4e94\u516d\u56db\
         +u5929\u65e5])", text):                                         
      44 +        target_wd = _WEEKDAY_ZH.get(m.group(1))                
      45 +        if target_wd is not None:                              
      46 +            days_ahead = (target_wd - now.weekday() + 7) % 7   
      47 +            if days_ahead == 0:                                
      48 +                days_ahead = 7                                 
      49 +            base = (now + timedelta(days=days_ahead)).replace(h
         +our=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)                      
      50 +    # дёӢдёӘжңҲ                                                   
      51 +    elif text.startswith("дёӢдёӘжңҲ"):                            
      52 +        month = now.month + 1                                  
      53 +        year = now.year + (1 if month > 12 else 0)             
      54 +        month = month if month <= 12 else month - 12           
      55 +        base = now.replace(year=year, month=month, day=1, hour=
         +0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)                          
      56 +                                                               
      57 +    if base is None:                                           
      58 +        return None                                            
      59 +                                                               
      60 +    # Apply time-of-day suffix                                 
      61 +    if "дёӢеҚҲ" in text:                                         
      62 +        base = base.replace(hour=14)                           
      63 +    elif "дёҠеҚҲ" in text:                                       
      64 +        base = base.replace(hour=9)                            
      65 +    elif "жҷҡдёҠ" in text:                                       
      66 +        base = base.replace(hour=20)                           
      67 +                                                               
      68 +    return base                                                
      69 +                                                               
      70 +

      72  async def handle_create_task(ctx: TurnContext) -> HandlerResult

      73      title = ctx.routing.params.get("title")

вқҜ let's dicuss SOAP mapping imprecise вҖ” Chinese outpatient records              
(гҖҠз—…еҺҶд№ҰеҶҷеҹәжң¬и§„иҢғгҖӢ) differ from Western SOAP what's next?                    

вҸә Good question. Let me analyze what's actually happening vs what the AI models
  flagged.

вҸә Here's my analysis вҖ” the situation is better than the AI models suggested.

  The "problem" is mostly a labeling mismatch, not a structural one

  Your 14 fields already ARE the гҖҠз—…еҺҶд№ҰеҶҷеҹәжң¬и§„иҢғгҖӢ standard. The schema.py
  docstring says it explicitly:

  в–Һ 14 fields per гҖҠз—…еҺҶд№ҰеҶҷеҹәжң¬и§„иҢғгҖӢ(еҚ«еҢ»ж”ҝеҸ‘гҖ”2010гҖ•11еҸ·) outpatient record 
  standard.

  The fields вҖ” дё»иҜү, зҺ°з—…еҸІ, ж—ўеҫҖеҸІ, иҝҮж•ҸеҸІ, дёӘдәәеҸІ, е©ҡиӮІеҸІ, е®¶ж—ҸеҸІ, дҪ“ж јжЈҖжҹҘ,
  дё“з§‘жЈҖжҹҘ, иҫ…еҠ©жЈҖжҹҘ, еҲқжӯҘиҜҠж–ӯ, жІ»з–—ж–№жЎҲ, еҢ»еҳұеҸҠйҡҸи®ҝ вҖ” are the correct Chinese
  outpatient record fields. You're NOT using Western SOAP structure.

  The only issue is that prompts and code comments call them "SOAP" as a
  grouping shorthand:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  в”Ӯ diagnosis.md   в”Ӯ "иҫ“е…Ҙ SOAP:"                                            в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  This is problematic because:
  1. It confuses LLMs вҖ” Qwen3/DeepSeek trained on Western medical data associate
   "SOAP" with a specific 4-section format, not 14 fields
  2. It confuses AI reviewers вҖ” all 5 models flagged this because they assumed
  you meant literal SOAP
  3. It confuses developers вҖ” "SOAP Assessment" вү  "еҲқжӯҘиҜҠж–ӯ" (Chinese diagnosis
  can include еҫ…жҺ’, иҖғиҷ‘, differential)

  What's actually correct already

  - The 14 field names and their Chinese labels
  - The field ordering (matches гҖҠз—…еҺҶд№ҰеҶҷеҹәжң¬и§„иҢғгҖӢ)
  - The extraction logic

  What to fix

  Option A (minimal, recommended): Replace "SOAP" label in LLM-facing prompts
  with the actual Chinese standard reference. Keep SOAP in code comments as
  developer shorthand.

  In prompts:
  - ## еҸҜз”Ёеӯ—ж®өпјҲSOAPпјү вҶ’ ## еҸҜз”Ёеӯ—ж®өпјҲй—ЁиҜҠз—…еҺҶж ҮеҮҶпјү
  - ### S вҖ” дё»и§Ӯ вҶ’ ### з—…еҸІ
  - ### O вҖ” е®ўи§Ӯ вҶ’ ### жЈҖжҹҘ
  - ### A вҖ” иҜ„дј° вҶ’ ### иҜҠж–ӯ
  - ### P вҖ” и®ЎеҲ’ вҶ’ ### еӨ„зҪ®
  - "з»“жһ„еҢ–SOAPз—…еҺҶи®°еҪ•" вҶ’ "з»“жһ„еҢ–й—ЁиҜҠз—…еҺҶ"

  Option B (thorough): Also rename in code comments (records.py,
  query_record.py) and schema references. Bigger diff, same benefit.

  ---
  My take: Option A is the right move. The field structure is already correct вҖ”
  you just need to stop telling the LLM it's "SOAP" so it doesn't apply Western
  assumptions. Code comments are for developers who already understand the
  shorthand.

  Want me to do Option A?

        5  ## How it works
        6  
        7 -- `utils/prompt_loader.py` reads files by key: `get_prompt("st
          -ructuring")` вҶ’ `prompts/structuring.md`                       
        7 +- `utils/prompt_loader.py` reads files by key: `get_prompt("in
          +tent/structuring")` вҶ’ `prompts/intent/structuring.md`         
        8  - Files are cached in memory on first read; call `invalidate()
           ` to reload
        9 -- Agent prompts (`doctor-agent.md`, `patient-agent.md`) are lo
          -aded by `build_prompt(role)` and injected into the LangChain `
          -ChatPromptTemplate`                                           
       10 -- Tool-internal prompts (`structuring.md`, `patient-interview.
          -md`) are loaded inside `@tool` functions for specialized LLM c
          -alls                                                          
        9 +- `prompt_composer.py` assembles the 6-layer prompt stack (sys
          +tem вҶ’ common вҶ’ intent вҶ’ knowledge вҶ’ context вҶ’ user)           
       10 +- `{current_date}` is auto-injected by the composer at runtime
       11  
       12  ## Architecture
       13  
       14 -### Agent Pipeline                                            
       14 +### Prompt Assembly (6-Layer Stack)                           
       15  
       16 -```mermaid                                                    
       17 -flowchart TD                                                  
       18 -    subgraph Channels                                         
       19 -        WEB[Web Channel]                                      
       20 -        WX[WeChat Channel]                                    
       21 -    end                                                       
       22 -                                                              
       23 -    HT["handle_turn(text, role, identity)"]                   
       24 -    FP{"Fast path?<br/>greeting / confirm"}                   
       25 -    FR["Fast reply<br/>0 LLM calls"]                          
       26 -                                                              
       27 -    WEB --> HT                                                
       28 -    WX --> HT                                                 
       29 -    HT --> FP                                                 
       30 -    FP -- yes --> FR                                          
       31 -                                                              
       32 -    subgraph Doctor Agent                                     
       33 -        DA["AgentExecutor<br/>doctor-agent.md"]               
       34 -        DA --> QR[query_records]                              
       35 -        DA --> LP[list_patients]                              
       36 -        DA --> LT[list_tasks]                                 
       37 -        DA --> CR[create_record]                              
       38 -        DA --> UR[update_record]                              
       39 -        DA --> CT[create_task]                                
       40 -    end                                                       
       41 -                                                              
       42 -    subgraph Patient Agent                                    
       43 -        PA["AgentExecutor<br/>patient-agent.md"]              
       44 -        PA --> AI[advance_interview]                          
       45 -    end                                                       
       46 -                                                              
       47 -    FP -- "role=doctor" --> DA                                
       48 -    FP -- "role=patient" --> PA                               
       49 -                                                              
       50 -    DA -- reply --> HT                                        
       51 -    PA -- reply --> HT                                        
       16  ```
       17 +Layer 1: system/base.md           вҖ” identity, safety, preceden
          +ce                                                            
       18 +Layer 2: common/{specialty}.md    вҖ” specialty knowledge (e.g.,
          + neurology)                                                   
       19 +Layer 3: intent/{intent}.md       вҖ” action-specific rules + ex
          +amples                                                        
       20 +Layer 4: Doctor knowledge (DB)    вҖ” auto-loaded from knowledge
          + base                                                         
       21 +Layer 5: Patient context (DB)     вҖ” records, history          
       22 +Layer 6: User message             вҖ” doctor's actual input     
       23 +```

вҸә Done. Now for #2 вҖ” let me explain:

  The patient-interview.md prompt tells the LLM:

  в–Һ еҪ“ chief_complaint + present_illness + з¬¬дәҢйҳ¶ж®ө4йЎ№еқҮе·Іж”¶йӣҶпјҢи®ҫзҪ® complete: 
  true

  This means the LLM is supposed to output "complete": true in its JSON response
   when all 7 fields are collected. But the Pydantic response model
  (InterviewLLMResponse) is what instructor/structured_call validates against.
  If that model doesn't have a complete field, one of two things happens:

  1. instructor strips it вҖ” the LLM outputs complete: true but instructor
  ignores it since it's not in the schema. The field is silently lost.
  2. instructor errors вҖ” if configured strictly, it rejects the extra field.

  Let me check if InterviewLLMResponse has complete:

  Searched for 1 pattern (ctrl+o to expand)

вҸә No complete field in the response model. So here's what's happening:

  The prompt tells the LLM to output complete: true, but the code ignores it.
  Instead, completeness is checked server-side via check_completeness(collected,
   mode=mode) вҖ” which looks at accumulated fields across all turns, not the
  LLM's self-assessment.

  This is actually fine as-is. The server-side check is more reliable than
  trusting the LLM to correctly decide when all fields are collected. The
  prompt's complete: true instruction is vestigial вҖ” the LLM might output it,
  but instructor strips it, and the code uses its own logic.

  No fix needed вҖ” the architecture is correct (server determines completeness,
  not LLM). If anything, the prompt instruction could be removed to avoid
  confusing the model, but it's harmless since instructor drops unknown fields.
